## Zombie fires in the Arctic smolder underground and refuse to die—what's causing them?
 - [https://phys.org/news/2024-05-zombie-arctic-smolder-underground-die.html](https://phys.org/news/2024-05-zombie-arctic-smolder-underground-die.html)
 - RSS feed: 
 - date published: 2024-05-29T17:18:03.424234+00:00

So-called "zombie fires" in the peatlands of Alaska, Canada and Siberia disappear from the Earth's surface and smolder underground during the winter before coming back to life the following spring. These fires puzzle scientists because they appear in early May, way ahead of the usual fire season in the far north, and can reignite for a number of years.

## YouTube's comments section: Political echo chamber or constructive cross-partisan forum?
 - [https://phys.org/news/2024-05-youtube-comments-section-political-echo.html](https://phys.org/news/2024-05-youtube-comments-section-political-echo.html)
 - RSS feed: 
 - date published: 2024-05-29T00:00:00+00:00

The YouTube comments sections of politically neutral news outlets might be more conducive to cooperative, cross-partisan conversation than their liberal and conservative counterparts, according to a study published May 29, 2024 in the open-access journal PLOS ONE by Seung Woo Chae and Sung Hyun Lee from Indiana University.

Mika Zibanejad, who remains scoreless through four games of the Eastern Conference Finals, committed a turnover in overtime that led to a penalty and the eventual winning goal for the Florida Panthers Tuesday, in their 3-2 win over the New York Rangers.
